INTRODUCTION AND SCOPE</b></h2><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">This privacy policy (this “Privacy Policy”) covers and describes how Fastly, Inc. and its subsidiaries (“Fastly”, “We” or “Us”) collect, use, share, secure and disclose the personal data we collect from individuals who interact with www.fastly.com and our websites that link to this Privacy Policy or who initiate communications with us (“Visitors”), individuals who register for or authenticate to our edge cloud services (“Customers”), individuals who register for or attend our marketing events or receive our marketing emails (“Attendees”) and individuals who submit an application for a career opportunity at Fastly (“Job Applicants”). </p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">Our websites, apps and services are designed for businesses and their representatives. We do not target consumers – individuals who seek to use products and services for their personal or household use.  Accordingly, we treat all personal data we collect as pertaining to individuals in their business capacity and not their individual capacity.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id=""><i>Our Edge Cloud Services/Fastly as a Data Processor or Service Provider.</i>  </p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">In their use of our services, Customers submit content, configurations and credentials to the Fastly edge cloud services to be processed. The security and privacy practices governing our Customers’ (and our Customers’ Internet clients’) use of our services and how we store, process, transmit and disclose the data submitted to the services by our Customers are described in and governed by our service contracts with our Customers. Our terms of service are available <a href="https://www.fastly.com/terms" id="here"><u>here</u></a>. Our data processing terms are available <a href="https://www.fastly.com/data-processing" id="here"><u>here</u></a>. To the extent a Customer submits to the services the personal data of European persons (including the United Kingdom and Switzerland) or other persons who are protected by similar data privacy laws, Fastly processes that personal data as a data processor or as the Customer’s sub-processor (as the case may be). Customers are solely responsible for establishing the policies governing, and ensuring compliance with all applicable laws and regulations related to, the Customer’s (and the Customer’s Internet client’s) collection and submission of personal data to our services. Any personal data about an individual (i.e., a “data subject”) hosted, stored or published by a Customer is the responsibility of the Customer and is not covered by this Privacy Policy.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">Fastly acknowledges that you may have the right to access your personal data. Fastly has no direct relationship with the data subjects whose personal data we process on behalf of our Customers. An individual who seeks to access, correct, amend, or delete personal data about them that we process on behalf of our Customers should direct their requests or queries to our Customer (i.e., the data controller. In addition, we will forward to the applicable Customer any request by a data subject received by Fastly regarding personal data processed on behalf of that Customer.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id=""><i>Fastly as a Data Controller </i></p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">Please read this Privacy Policy carefully to understand the categories and specific pieces of personal data we collect and how we collect, use, disclose, and protect the personal data of our Visitors, Customers, Attendees and Job Applicants, as well as the choices available to you regarding that information.  </p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id=""><i>International Data Transfers </i></p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">When Fastly operates as a data controller (i.e., when we determine the manner, purposes and means of the processing of others’ personal information), Fastly may collect from, transfer to, or process and store your personal information in the United States and other countries other than the country where you live. When we transfer personal data from the EU, Switzerland, or UK to any other country, we will do so according to an adequate mechanism of transfer.  </p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">Fastly has certified its services under the EU–U.S. Privacy Shield Framework and the Swiss-U.S. Privacy Shield Framework as set forth by the U.S. Department of Commerce and the European Union and Switzerland, respectively (collectively, the “Privacy Shield”). Although the Privacy Shield has been ruled invalid, Fastly adheres to the Privacy Shield Principles with respect to personal information we receive from Visitors, Customers or Attendees in the EU, the United Kingdom and Switzerland. You can view our notice of Privacy Shield self-certification <a href="https://www.fastly.com/privacy-shield-notice" id="here"><u>here</u></a>. For more information on the Privacy Shield, please visit the <a href="https://www.privacyshield.gov/" id="us-department-of-commerce-s-privacy-shield-website"><u>U.S. Department of Commerce’s Privacy Shield website</u></a>.</p><h2 class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-cZMNgc OtPyA" id="2-fastly-collection-and-use-of-personal-information"><b>2. FASTLY COLLECTION AND USE OF PERSONAL INFORMATION</b></h2><h3 class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-jUosCB CToUt" id="21-what-categories-and-specific-types-of-personal-data-does-fastly-collect?"><b>2.1. What categories and specific types of personal data does Fastly collect?</b></h3><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">Information that we collect from or about you includes the following:</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id=""><span><table>
<tr><th><strong>Categories of collected personal data</strong></th>
<th><strong>Description</strong></th></tr>
<tr><td>Identification and Contact Information</td>
<td>Details such as name, postal address, e-mail address, or telephone number, either actively or passively, and billing information such as credit card number and tax address.</td></tr>
<tr><td>Professional Information</td>
<td>Information that you provide when you fill in forms on our websites, such as your job title, credit card number and other contact details. Information you provide as a contributing user that is published or displayed (hereafter, referred to as “posted”) on public areas of our websites, or transmitted to other users of our websites or third parties. Your user contributions are posted and may be accessed by others at your own risk.Information you provide when applying for a job with Fastly, including your résumé.</td></tr>
<tr><td>Transactional Data</td>
<td>Details of financial transactions you carry out through our websites or related to orders of our services, such as credit card information, or in connection with planning and hosting corporate events, such as reservations and hospitality.</td></tr>
<tr><td>Technical Data</td>
<td>Information about your Internet connection and Internet protocol (IP) address, your login data, the equipment you use to access our websites, time zone settings and location, browser plug-in types and versions, operating system and other technology on the devices you use to access or use our websites.</td></tr>
<tr><td>Marketing and Communications Data</td>
<td>Your preferences in receiving marketing from us and our partners and your communication preferences and consents. Your responses to surveys that we might ask you to complete for research purposes.Records and copies of your correspondence (including e-mail addresses, IRC handles, and Twitter handles), if you contact us. This information may contain contact details you include within your correspondence.</td></tr>
<tr><td>Behavioral Data</td>
<td>Inferred or assumed information relating to your behavior and interests, based on your online activity and your use of our websites.</td></tr>
</table></span></p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">We do not collect any “Special Categories of Personal Data” about you. This includes details about your race or ethnicity, religious or philosophical beliefs, sex life, sexual orientation, political opinions, trade union membership, information about your health and genetic and biometric data. We do not collect any information about criminal convictions and offenses.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id=""><i>Legal Basis and Purpose for Processing Personal Data </i></p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">Where we process personal data as a processor or a service provider pursuant to service contracts with our Customers, we process personal data on the instructions of the Customer, and only as necessary, appropriate and customary to provide our services.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">If you are an individual located in the European Economic Area (EEA) or an individual whose personal data is protected by laws similar to the GDPR, our legal basis and purpose for collecting and using the personal data described in Section 2.1 above will depend on the personal data concerned and the specific context in which we collect it. However, we will normally collect personal data from you only where: (a) we have your consent to do so, (b) where we need the personal data to perform a contract with you (e.g. to deliver the services you have requested), or (c) where the processing is in our or a third party’s legitimate interests (and not overridden by your data protection interests or fundamental rights and freedoms). In some cases, we may also have a legal obligation to collect personal data from you or may otherwise need the personal data to protect your vital interests or those of another person.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id=""><i>Examples of Legitimate Basis and Purpose for Collecting Your Personal Data</i></p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">In connection with your use of our services, we collect and process personal data to perform our contractual obligations related to the services that you have requested. Where we collect personal data in connection with operating our websites and services, we have a legitimate interest in ensuring our websites, services and associated networks and IT systems operate properly and securely. Where you have requested to receive information about our products, services and business or other marketing communications, then we process personal data based upon our legitimate interest in engaging in direct marketing with Visitors, Customers, Attendees, individuals and companies that have requested to receive information from us. </p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">Where you have responded to a job posting on our websites, we collect and process personal data as part of our consideration of your application. Where we rely on your consent to process the personal data, you have the right to withdraw or decline your consent at any time. Please note that this does not affect the lawfulness of the processing based on consent before its withdrawal. </p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">Where we collect data about online behavior, including through the use of cookies, we have a legitimate interest in providing you with an optimal user experience and understanding and analyzing how Visitors interact with our website. You can find more the use of cookies in the websites, please read and review our Cookie Policy found <a href="https://www.fastly.com/cookies" id="here"><u>here</u></a>.</p><h3 class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-jUosCB CToUt" id="22-how-does-fastly-collect-my-personal-data?"><b>2.2 How does Fastly collect my personal data?</b></h3><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">Fastly collects your information both actively and passively (in accordance with our Cookie Policy) as you interact with our websites or contact us.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">Fastly may directly collect personal data you provide us in the following ways:</p><ul><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">When you complete forms on our websites, such as registering an account, subscribing to a service, posting a comment or applying for a job.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">When you create an account to use our services or create a new user for that account.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">When you complete transactions through our websites, such as fulfilling an order for our services.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">When you perform search queries on our websites.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">When you post messages on our websites, either in public areas or directly to other users or third parties.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">When you use our publicly accessible blogs.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">When you contact us outside of our websites, such as via email or Twitter.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">When you request assistance from our Support team.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">When you respond to surveys we ask you to complete for research purposes.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">When you provide information that will be posted published or displayed on public areas of our websites.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">When you transmit information to other users of our websites or third parties as a user contribution.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">When you register for or attend our Marketing Activities.</p></li></ul><h3 class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-jUosCB CToUt" id="23-does-fastly-collect-personal-data-automatically?"><b>2.3 Does Fastly collect personal data automatically?</b></h3><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">As is true of most websites and services provided using the Internet, we gather certain information automatically. This information may include Internet protocol (IP) addresses, browser type, Internet service provider (ISP), the referring page that you navigated to our websites from, the page that you navigated to from our websites, the files viewed on our site (e.g. HTML pages, graphics, etc.), operating system, date/time stamp, and/or clickstream data to analyze trends in the aggregate and administer the site.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">The information we collect automatically is statistical data, which we may associate with personal data we collect in other ways or receive from third parties. This information helps us to improve our websites and to deliver better and more personalized service.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">Fastly and our partners use cookies or similar technologies (such as web beacons) to gather information, analyze trends, administer our websites, track users’ movements around our websites, and to gather demographic information about our user base as a whole. These technologies may provide us with personal data, information about devices and networks you utilize to access our websites, analytics information and other information regarding your interactions with our websites. Users can control the use of cookies at the individual browser level but if you choose to disable cookies, it may limit your use of certain features or functions on our website or service. For detailed information about the use of cookies and related technologies in our websites, please read and review our Cookie Policy found <a href="https://www.fastly.com/cookies" id="here"><u>here</u></a>.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">We partner with a third party to manage our advertising on other sites. Our third party partner may use technologies such as cookies to gather information about your activities on our websites and other sites in order to provide you advertising based upon your browsing activities and interests. If you wish to not have this information used for the purpose of serving you interest-based ads, you may opt-out by clicking <a href="http://optout.aboutads.info/" id="here"><u>here</u></a> (or if located in the European Union, click <a href="https://www.youronlinechoices.eu/" id="here"><u>here</u></a>). Please note that this does not opt you out of being served ads. You will continue to receive generic ads.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">In connection with operating our global caching network’s general interaction with the Internet, Fastly collects client IP address information on a limited basis to provide and improve its services. Fastly also may collect and retain for its legitimate business purposes client or Customer IP addresses associated with suspicious activity that may pose a risk to the Fastly network or our Customers, or that are associated with administrative connections to the Fastly service.</p><h3 class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-jUosCB CToUt" id="24-how-does-fastly-use-my-personal-data?"><b>2.4 How does Fastly use my personal data?</b></h3><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">We use your information to enhance your experience using our websites and services.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">We use personal data that we collect about you or that you provide to us, including any personal data about Visitors, Customers and Attendees:</p><ul><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">To present our websites and their contents to you.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">To provide you with access to our services and to maintain access controls over secured areas of our websites.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">To provide you services for which you have engaged us.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">To provide you with information, products, or services that you request from us, including technical instructions for implementing your service and responding to customer support and sales inquiries.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">To fulfill any purpose for which you provide it.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">To provide you with notices about your account and/or subscription, including expiration and renewal notices.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">To notify you about changes to our websites or any products or services, which include changes to our documentation, other technical and administrative notices, security advisories and other alerts that you may subscribe for on our websites.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">To provide you with information or services that you request from us.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">To carry out our obligations and enforce our rights arising from any contracts entered into between you and us, including for billing, collection and completing credit card transactions.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">To save your preferences (including requests to not receive communications).</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">To allow you to participate in interactive features on our websites.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">To personalize our websites to optimize your experience and match your preferences.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">To send you promotional materials about our services and events, including newsletters, product updates, information about and invitations to marketing events.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">To process and deliver contest or sweepstakes entries and rewards.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">To plan and host Marketing Activities.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">To communicate with you about corporate marketing events, which may include promotional information.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">In any way we describe when you provide or we collect the information.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">To comply with applicable legal and regulatory requirements.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">For any other purpose with your consent.</p></li></ul><h3 class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-jUosCB CToUt" id="25-how-long-does-fastly-retain-my-information?"><b>2.5 How long does Fastly retain my information?</b></h3><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">We retain your information for as long as your account is active or as needed to provide you our services or perform our contractual obligations, unless a longer retention period is required or permitted by law. The retention period shall not exceed the duration of our business relationship with you plus (7) years unless we have a legitimate business interest need to retain the information for a longer period, which include maintaining a record of your preferences, securing the integrity of databases, conducting audits, complying with our legal and contractual obligations, resolving disputes, and enforcing our agreements.</p><h2 class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-cZMNgc OtPyA" id="3-third-party-collection-and-use-of-personal-data"><b>3. THIRD PARTY COLLECTION AND USE OF PERSONAL DATA</b></h2><h3 class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-jUosCB CToUt" id="31-does-fastly-share-my-personal-data-with-others?"><b>3.1 Does Fastly share my personal data with others?</b></h3><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id=""><b>Third-Party Service Providers</b></p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">We engage third-party service providers in the operation of our business or to support our business. We consequently share information, including personal data, with these contracted third-party service providers in connection with using their services. These include cloud-based productivity and collaboration tools, customer relations management, staffing service providers, backup, storage, payment processing, analytics and other services. We also engage and share information with third-party service providers for fraud protection, credit risk reduction and payment collection associated with our accounts. Our service providers may have access to, process or store your personal data for the purpose of providing us with their contracted-for services. </p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">Our service providers are not authorized to process your personal data for purposes other than as necessary, appropriate or reasonable to provide the service we have purchased.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id=""><b>Affiliates</b></p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">We share information, including personal data, with our subsidiaries and affiliates in the operation of our global business because our subsidiaries and affiliates may provide you services under our contracts or other functions, consistent with the purposes described in Section 2.4 above.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id=""><b>Third Party Cookies</b></p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">As described in our Cookie Policy, we collect and share information through the use of cookies.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id=""><b>Consent</b></p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">We may disclose your personal data to any third party with your consent.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id=""><b>Compliance with Laws; Law Enforcement Requests; Protection of Our Rights</b></p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">In certain situations, we may be required to disclose personal data in response to lawful requests by public authorities, including to meet law enforcement requirements. We may disclose personal data to respond to subpoenas, court orders, or legal process, or to establish or exercise our legal rights or defend against legal claims. We may also share such information if we believe it is necessary or appropriate in order to protect our rights, property, or safety of Fastly, our Visitors, Customers or Attendees, Job Applicants, our personnel or others, to investigate, prevent, or take action regarding illegal activities, suspected fraud, situations involving potential threats to the physical safety of any person, violations of our contracts, or as otherwise required by law.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id=""><b>Corporate Events</b></p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">We may share your personal data to a potential buyer or other successor in the event of a merger, divestiture, restructuring, reorganization, dissolution, or other sale or transfer of some or all of Fastly’s assets, whether as a going concern or as part of bankruptcy, liquidation or similar proceeding, in which personal data held by Fastly about our websites users is among the assets transferred. We may also share your personal data with potential investors, financing sources, auditors or agents that may conduct due diligence of our business. You will be notified via email and/or a prominent notice on our websites of any change in ownership or uses of your personal data, as well as any choices you may have regarding your personal data.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id=""><b>Referrals</b></p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">Our services permit you to refer our services to other people, including, for instance, to add users to your account. If you provide us with contact information for persons you would like to refer, we will communicate with the referred persons and may disclose you as the source of the referral. If you believe that one of your contacts has provided us with your personal data and you would like to request that it be removed from our databases, please contact us at <a href="mailto:abuse@fastly.com" id="abuse@fastlycom">abuse@fastly.com</a>. Fastly’s language for official communications is English.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id=""><b>Community Forums</b></p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">Our website includes a community forum and other interactive features. When interacting in the community form, your account is publicly accessible unless you change the privacy settings of your profile through your account portal.</p><h3 class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-jUosCB CToUt" id="32-do-third-parties-collect-my-personal-data?"><b>3.2 Do third parties collect my personal data?</b></h3><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">Some content or applications are served by third parties, including advertisers, ad networks and servers, content providers, and application providers who may collect your information as you interact with those parties through our websites.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">This collection can occur under the following circumstances:</p><ul><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">When you log in to our websites using sign-in services such as Facebook Connect or an Open ID provider.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">When you use social media features, such as the Facebook Like button, and widgets, such as the Share button or interactive mini-programs that run on our site. These features may collect your IP address, which page you are visiting on our websites, and may set a cookie to enable the feature to function properly. These social media features are either hosted by a third party or hosted directly on our websites.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">You can log in to our websites using sign-in services such as Facebook Connect or an Open ID provider. These services authenticate your identity and provide you the option to share certain personal data with us such as your name and email address to pre-populate our sign up form. Services like Facebook Connect give you the option to post information about your activities on our websites to your profile page to share with others within your network.</p></li></ul><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">These third parties may also use automatic data collection technologies such as cookies or beacons to collect information about you when you use our websites, your online activities, and across different websites and other online services. They may use this information to provide you with interest-based (behavioral) advertising or other targeted content.</p><h3 class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-jUosCB CToUt" id="33-data-supplementation"><b>3.3 Data Supplementation</b></h3><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">We may receive information about you from other sources, including publicly available databases or third parties from whom we have purchased data, and combine this data with information we already have about you. This helps us to update, expand and analyze our records, identify new customers, and provide products and services that may be of interest to you. If you provide us personal data about others, or if others give us your information, we will only use that information for the specific reason for which it was provided to us. If we receive personal data about individuals from a third party in order to engage in marketing of our services, then we will market to those individuals only in their capacity as representatives of companies we wish to sell to and we will present you an opportunity to opt-out of future communications.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">Examples of the types of personal data that may be obtained from public sources or purchased from third parties and combined with information we already have about you, may include:</p><ul><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">Contact information about you, including your name, email address telephone number, from third party sources to verify your address so we can properly prevent fraud or communicate with you; or</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">Data purchased from third parties, such as social networking sites and conference attendee lists, that is combined with information we already have about you, to create more tailored advertising and products. If you receive a marketing communication or promotion from us, you may opt-out of these communications at any time by clicking the unsubscribe link provided in the email or by sending a request to abuse@fastly.com.</p></li></ul><h3 class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-jUosCB CToUt" id="34-how-is-my-personal-data-handled-by-third-party-sites?"><b>3.4 How is my personal data handled by third-party sites?</b></h3><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">Our websites may include links to other websites whose privacy practices may differ from those of Fastly. If you submit personal data to any of those sites, your information is governed by their privacy policies. We encourage you to carefully read the privacy policy of any website you visit.</p><h2 class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-cZMNgc OtPyA" id="4-your-choices-and-rights"><b>4. YOUR CHOICES AND RIGHTS</b></h2><h3 class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-jUosCB CToUt" id="41-how-can-i-limit-how-my-information-is-used-and-disclosed?"><b>4.1 How can I limit how my information is used and disclosed?</b></h3><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">You can use certain web browser and opt-out options to limit the personal data you provide us.  We cannot guarantee the effectiveness of these third-party controls.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">The following mechanisms are in place to provide control over your information by:</p><ul><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id=""><b>Turning off tracking technologies and advertising</b>. As described in our Cookie Policy, you can set your browser to refuse all or some browser cookies, or to alert you when cookies are being set. If you disable or refuse cookies, please note that some parts of our websites may become inaccessible or not function properly.</p></li><li><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id=""><b>Opting out</b>. If you have subscribed to our newsletter(s), you can choose to stop receiving marketing emails, such as our newsletter or new product announcements, by following the unsubscribe instructions included in these emails or by contacting us at <a href="mailto:abuse@fastly.com" id="abuse@fastlycom"><u>abuse@fastly.com</u></a> .</p></li></ul><h3 class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-jUosCB CToUt" id="42-how-can-i-correct-or-remove-my-personal-data?"><b>4.2 How can I correct or remove my personal data?</b></h3><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">If you want to review, delete, or change your personal data, you can log in to the appropriate website and visit your account profile page. After you log in, you can send us an e-mail at the address noted in the Contact Information section below to request access to, correction of, or deletion of any personal data that you provided to us. You can also request the closure of your account within your account settings. If we fulfill your request to close your account, we will remove your user account from our active database and your account will be archived as an inactive account. We retain your account information in accordance with our retention policy as described above in Section 2.5 and in order to maintain a record of your preferences, to secure the integrity of applicable databases, conduct audits, comply with our legal and contractual obligations, resolve disputes, and enforce our agreements.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">To remove your personal data from our blog, please follow the instructions to <a href="https://help.disqus.com/customer/portal/articles/466229-removing-and-editing-your-comments" id="remove-posts"><u>remove posts</u></a> or <a href="https://help.disqus.com/customer/portal/articles/472013-deleting-your-account" id="delete-your-user-account"><u>delete your user account</u></a>. If you want your personal data removed from other places on our websites, please contact us via the information supplied in the <b>Contact Information</b> section below.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">Upon request, we will provide you with information about whether we hold, or process on behalf of a third party, any of your personal data or if we have retained your personal data after the closure of your account.  To request this information please contact us via the information supplied in the Contact Information section below. We will respond to your request within the timeframe specified by applicable law.</p><h3 class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-jUosCB CToUt" id="43-how-can-i-report-abuse?"><b>4.3 How can I report abuse?</b></h3><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">If you need to report abuse, please contact us by email at a<a href="mailto:abuse@fastly.com" id="buse@fastlycom">buse@fastly.com.</a> Fastly’s language for official communications is English.</p><h2 class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-cZMNgc OtPyA" id="5-security-and-privacy-measures"><b>5. SECURITY AND PRIVACY MEASURES</b></h2><h3 class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-jUosCB CToUt" id="51-how-does-fastly-protect-my-information-and-data?"><b>5.1 How does Fastly protect my information and data?</b></h3><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">We have implemented measures designed to secure your personal data from accidental loss and from unauthorized access, use, alteration, and disclosure.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">Information you provide to us is stored on our secure servers behind firewalls. Any sensitive information is encrypted using Transport Layer Security (TLS) (sometimes referred to as Secure Sockets Layer or SSL).</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">You must also make sure that your personal data is safe and secure. Even if we give you (or you have chosen) a password for access to certain parts of our websites, you are responsible for keeping this password confidential. Do not share your password with anyone. We urge you to be careful about giving out information in public areas of our websites, for example, message boards. The personal data you share in public areas may be viewed by any user of our websites.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">Information that is transmitted via the Internet is not completely secure. We cannot guarantee the security of your personal data transmitted to our websites. Any transmission of personal data is at your own risk. We are not responsible if you circumvent any privacy settings or security measures on our websites.</p><h3 class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-jUosCB CToUt" id="52-how-does-fastly-limit-access-to-my-personal-data?"><b>5.2 How does Fastly limit access to my personal data?</b></h3><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">We limit access to certain pages on our websites and allow you to set certain privacy settings via your account profile; however, be aware that no security measures are perfect or impenetrable.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">Additionally, we cannot control the actions of other users of our websites with whom you may choose to share your user contributions. Given that, we cannot and do not guarantee that your user contributions will not be viewed by unauthorized persons.</p><h2 class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-cZMNgc OtPyA" id="6-other-important-information"><b>6. OTHER IMPORTANT INFORMATION</b></h2><h3 class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-jUosCB CToUt" id="61-children-under-the-age-of-16"><b>6.1 Children Under the Age of 16</b></h3><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">Our websites are not intended for children under 16 years of age. No one under age 16 may provide any personal data to or on the websites.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">We do not knowingly collect personal data from children under 16. If you are under 16, do not use or provide any information on our websites or on or through any of their features, register on the websites, make any purchases through the websites, use any of the interactive or public comment features of our websites or provide any information about yourself to us, including your name, address, telephone number, e-mail address or any screen name or user name you may use. If we learn we have collected or received personal data from a child under 16, we will delete that information immediately.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">If you believe we might have any information from or about a child under 16, please contact us via the Contact Information section below.</p><h3 class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-jUosCB CToUt" id="62-california-privacy-rights"><b>6.2 California Privacy Rights</b></h3><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">California Civil Code Section § 1798.83 permits users of our websites that are California residents to request certain information regarding our disclosure of personal data to third parties for their direct marketing purposes. To make such a request, please send an e-mail or write us at our mailing address noted in the Contact Information section below.</p><h2 class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-cZMNgc OtPyA" id="7-contact-information"><b>7. CONTACT INFORMATION</b></h2><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id=""> If you have any questions or comments about this Privacy Policy and our privacy practices, contact us at: <a href="mailto:abuse@fastly.com" id="abuse@fastlycom">abuse@fastly.com</a>. Fastly’s language for official communications is English.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">or Fastly, Inc., Attn: General Counsel and SVP of Trust, 475 Brannan St, Suite 300 San Francisco, CA 94107.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">If you have an unresolved privacy or data use concern that we have not addressed satisfactorily, you may contact our U.S.-based third party dispute resolution provider (free of charge) at: <a href="https://feedback-form.truste.com/watchdog/request" id="https//feedback-formtrustecom/watchdog/request"><u>https://feedback-form.truste.com/watchdog/request</u></a>.</p><h2 class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-cZMNgc OtPyA" id="8-changes-to-this-privacy-policy"><b>8. CHANGES TO THIS PRIVACY POLICY</b></h2><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf" id="">It is our policy to post any changes we make to this Privacy Policy on this page with a notice on <a href="http://docs.fastly.com/changes" id="http//docsfastlycom/changes"><u>http://docs.fastly.com/changes</u></a><u> </u>that this Privacy Policy has been updated. If we make material changes to how we treat our users’ personal data, we will notify you by e-mail to the primary e-mail address specified in your account and/or through a notice on <a href="http://docs.fastly.com/changes" id="http//docsfastlycom/changes"><u>http://docs.fastly.com/changes</u></a> thirty (30) days prior to the change becoming effective. We reserve the right to change this Privacy Policy without thirty (30) days’ notice for the purpose of complying with applicable law. The date this Privacy Policy was last revised is identified at the top of the page and will be reviewed, and revised if required, in accordance with applicable law. You are responsible for ensuring we have an up-to-date active and deliverable e-mail address for you and for periodically visiting <a href="http://docs.fastly.com/changes" id="http//docsfastlycom/changes"><u>http://docs.fastly.com/changes</u></a> and this Privacy Policy to check for any changes.</p><p class="sc-bTfYFJ sc-kHOZwM renderer__RTBodyCopy-sc-10o88w8-0 bIGkTf"
